\\begin{aligned}\n   158→            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n   159→            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\: &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n   164→            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                         \\\\\n   165→            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\n   166→            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   \\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\n   169→            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\lambda \\neq 0                                           \\\\\n   170→            &\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda  \\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\n   171→            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\mu \\neq 0 &\\hspace{15mm} \\textbf{b}_t \\leftarrow g_t                                           \\\\\n   176→            &\\hspace{10mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{nesterov}                                       \\\\\n   177→            &\\hspace{15mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_{t} + \\mu \\textbf{b}_t                               \\\\\n   178→            &\\hspace{10mm}\\textbf{else}                                                   \\\\[-1.ex]\n   179→            &\\hspace{15mm} g_t  \\leftarrow  \\textbf{b}_t                                         \\\\\n   180→            &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n   183→            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n   184→       \\end{aligned}\n   185→\n   186→    Nesterov momentum is based on the formula from\n   187→    `On the importance of initialization and momentum in deep learning`__.\n   188→    \"\"\"\n   189→    + rf\"\"\"\n   190→    Args:\n   191→        {_params_doc}\n   192→        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3)\n   193→        momentum (float, (default: 0)\n   196→        nesterov (bool, optional): enables Nesterov momentum. Only applicable\n   197→            when momentum is non-zero. (default: False)\n   198→        {_maximize_doc}\n   199→        {_foreach_doc}\n   200→        {_differentiable_doc}\n   201→        {_fused_doc}\n   202→    \"\"\"\n   203→    + r\"\"\"\n   204→\n   205→    Example:\n   206→        >>> # xdoctest: +SKIP\n   207→        >>> optimizer = torch.optim.SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.1, momentum=0.9)\n   208→        >>> optimizer.zero_grad()\n   209→        >>> loss_fn(model(input), target).backward()\n   210→        >>> optimizer.step()\n   211→\n   212→    __ http://www.cs.toronto.edu/%7Ehinton/absps/momentum.pdf\n   213→\n   214→    .. note::\n   215→        The implementation of SGD with Momentum/Nesterov subtly differs from\n   216→        Sutskever et al. and implementations in some other frameworks.\n   217→\n   218→        Considering the specific case of Momentum, the update can be written as\n   219→\n   220→        .. math::\n   221→            \\begin{aligned}\n   222→                v_{t+1} & = \\mu * v_{t} + g_{t+1}, \\\\\n   223→                p_{t+1} & = p_{t} - \\text{lr} * v_{t+1},\n   224→            \\end{aligned}\n   225→\n   226→        where :math:`p`, :math:`g`, :math:`v` and :math:`\\mu` denote the\n   227→        parameters, gradient, velocity, and momentum respectively.\n   228→\n   229→        This is in contrast to Sutskever et al. and\n   230→        other frameworks which employ an update of the form\n   231→\n   232→        .. math::\n   233→            \\begin{aligned}\n   234→                v_{t+1} & = \\mu * v_{t} + \\text{lr} * g_{t+1}, \\\\\n   235→                p_{t+1} & = p_{t} - v_{t+1}.\n   236→            \\end{aligned}\n   237→\n   238→        The Nesterov version is analogously modified.\n   239→\n   240→        Moreover, the initial value of the momentum buffer is set to the\n   241→        gradient value at the first step. This is in contrast to some other\n   242→        frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\n   243→        of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\n   244→        by dampening. with momentum).\n\n    .. math::\n       \\begin{aligned}\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\: \\theta_0 \\text{ (params)}, \\: f(\\theta)\n                \\text{ (objective)}, \\: \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},                          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{13mm} \\:\\mu \\text{ (momentum)}, \\:\\tau \\text{ (dampening)},\n            \\:\\textit{ nesterov,}\\:\\textit{ maximize}                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do} (\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   \\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\lambda \\neq 0                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} g_t &\\hspace{10mm}\\textbf{if} \\: t > 1                                                   \\\\\n            &\\hspace{15mm} \\textbf{b}_t \\leftarrow \\mu \\textbf{b}_{t-1} + (1-\\tau) g_t           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\textbf{else}                                                          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{15mm} \\textbf{b}_t \\leftarrow g_t                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{nesterov}                                       \\\\\n            &\\hspace{15mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_{t} + \\mu \\textbf{b}_t                               \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\textbf{else}                                                   \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\hspace{15mm} g_t  \\leftarrow  \\textbf{b}_t                                         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1} - \\gamma g_t                    \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    Nesterov momentum is based on the formula from\n    `On the importance of initialization and momentum in deep learning`__.\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3)\n        momentum (float, optional): momentum factor (default: 0)\n        dampening (float, optional): dampening for momentum (default: 0)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        nesterov (bool, Only applicable\n            when momentum is non-zero. (default: False)\n        {_maximize_doc}\n        {_foreach_doc}\n        {_differentiable_doc}\n        {_fused_doc}\n    \"\"\"\n    + r\"\"\"\n\n    Example:\n        >>> # xdoctest: +SKIP\n        >>> optimizer = torch.optim.SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.1, momentum=0.9)\n        >>> optimizer.zero_grad()\n        >>> loss_fn(model(input), target).backward()\n        >>> optimizer.step()\n\n    __ http://www.cs.toronto.edu/%7Ehinton/absps/momentum.pdf\n\n    .. note::\n        The implementation of SGD with Momentum/Nesterov subtly differs from\n        Sutskever et al. and implementations in some other frameworks.\n\n        Considering the specific case of Momentum, the update can be written as\n\n        .. math::\n            \\begin{aligned}\n                v_{t+1} & = \\mu * v_{t} + g_{t+1}, \\\\\n                p_{t+1} & = p_{t} - \\text{lr} * v_{t+1},\n            \\end{aligned}\n\n        where :math:`p`, :math:`g`, :math:`v` and :math:`\\mu` denote the\n        parameters, gradient, velocity, and momentum respectively.\n\n        This is in contrast to Sutskever et al. and\n        other frameworks which employ an update of the form\n\n        .. math::\n            \\begin{aligned}\n                v_{t+1} & = \\mu * v_{t} + \\text{lr} * g_{t+1}, \\\\\n                p_{t+1} & = p_{t} - v_{t+1}.\n            \\end{aligned}\n\n        The Nesterov version is analogously modified.\n\n        Moreover, the initial value of the momentum buffer is set to the\n        gradient value at the first step. This is in contrast to some other\n        frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\n        of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\n        by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef sgd(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    d_p_list: list[Tensor],\n    momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\n    # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\n    # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\n    has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\n    foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\n    fused: Optional[bool] = None,\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    *,\n    weight_decay: float,\n    momentum: float,\n    lr: float,\n    dampening: float,\n    nesterov: bool,\n    maximize: bool,\n):\n    r\"\"\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\n\n    See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. We only want to change\n    # the default when neither have been user-specified. Note that we default to foreach\n    # and pass False to use_fused. This is not a mistake--we want to give the fused impl\n    # bake-in time before making it the default, even if it is typically faster.\n    if foreach is None and fused is None:\n        # why must we be explicit about an if statement for torch.jit.is_scripting here?\n        #                               \\\\\n   294→            &\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda  \\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\n   295→            &\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\n   296→            &\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\n   297→            &\\hspace{5mm}\\widehat{m_t} \\leftarrow   m_t/\\big(1-\\beta_1^t \\big)                   \\\\\n   298→            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\n   299→            &\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\leftarrow \\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\n   300→            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)              \\\\\n   301→            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n   302→            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow   v_t/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)                  \\\\\n   303→            &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1} - \\gamma \\widehat{m_t}/\n   304→                \\big(\\sqrt{\\widehat{v_t}} + \\epsilon \\big)                                       \\\\\n   305→            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n   306→            &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n   307→            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n   308→       \\end{aligned}\n   309→\n   310→    For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\n   311→    \"\"\"\n   312→    + rf\"\"\"\n   313→    Args:\n   314→        {_params_doc}\n   315→        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\n   316→            is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\n   317→            LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\n   318→        betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n   319→            running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n   320→        eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n   321→            numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n   322→        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n   323→        decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\n   324→            equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\n   325→            decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\n   326→        amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\n   327→            algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\n   328→            (default: False)\n   329→        {_foreach_doc}\n   330→        {_maximize_doc}\n   331→        {_capturable_doc}\n   332→        {_differentiable_doc}\n   333→        {_fused_doc}\n   334→    .. Note::\n   335→        A prototype implementation of Adam and AdamW for MPS supports `torch.float32` and `torch.float16`.\n   336→    .. _Adam\\: A Method for Stochastic Optimization:\n   337→        https://arxiv.org/abs/1412.6980\n   338→    .. _On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond:\n   339→        https://openreview.net/forum?id=ryQu7f-RZ\n   340→\n   341→    \"\"\"\n   342→)\n   343→\n   344→\n   345→def _single_tensor_adam(\n   346→    params: list[Tensor],\n   347→    grads: list[Tensor],\n   348→    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n   349→    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   350→    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   351→    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n   352→    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n   353→    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n   354→    *,\n   355→    amsgrad: bool,\n   356→    has_complex: bool,\n   357→    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n   358→    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n   359→    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n   360→    weight_decay: float,\n   361→    eps: float,\n   362→    maximize: bool,\n   363→    capturable: bool,\n   364→    differentiable: bool,\n   365→    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n   366→):\n   367→    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n   368→\n   369→    if torch.jit.is_scripting():\n   370→        # this assert is due to JIT being dumb and not realizing that the ops below\n   371→        # have overloads to handle both float and Tensor lrs, so we just assert it's\n   372→        # a float since most people using JIT are using floats\n   373→        assert isinstance(lr, float)\n   374→        assert isinstance(beta1, float)\n   375→        assert isinstance(beta2, float)\n   376→    else:\n   377→        lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n   378→        # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n   379→\n   380→    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor, otherwise, we prefer\n   381→    # treating it as a scalar.\n   382→    # Note: ensure type declaration is under conditional check for isinstance\n   383→    # or else torchscript will get cranky about the DeviceDict type.\n   384→    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n   385→        beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDtypeDict] = {(beta1.device, beta1.dtype): beta1}\n   386→    else:\n   387→        beta1_dict = None\n   388→\n   389→    for i, param in enumerate(params):\n   390→        grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\n   391→        exp_avg = exp_avgs[i]\n   392→        exp_avg_sq = exp_avg_sqs[i]\n   393→        step_t = state_steps[i]\n   394→\n   395→        # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n   396→        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n   397→            capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices()\n   398→            assert (\n   399→                param.device.type == step_t.device.type\n   400→                and param.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n   401→            ), (\n   402→                f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n   403→            )\n   404→\n   405→        # update step\n   406→        step_t += 1\n   407→\n   408→        if weight_decay != 0:\n   409→            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n   410→                # Perform stepweight decay\n   411→                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n   412→            else:\n   413→                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n   414→                if differentiable and isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n   415→                    if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n   416→                        grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n   417→                    else:\n   418→                        grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n   419→                else:\n   420→                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n   421→\n   422→        if torch.is_complex(param):\n   423→            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n   424→            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n   425→            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n   426→            if amsgrad:\n   427→                max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_real(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n   428→            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n   429→\n   430→        device = param.device\n   431→\n   432→        if beta1_dict is not None:\n   433→            dtype = param.dtype  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n   434→\n   435→            # cast to workaround https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/140601\n   436→            key = (device, dtype)\n   437→            if key not in beta1_dict:\n   438→                beta1_dict[key] = beta1.to(  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n   439→                    device=device, dtype=dtype, non_blocking=True\n   440→                )\n   441→\n   442→            device_beta1: Union[float, Tensor] = beta1_dict[key]\n   443→        else:\n   444→            device_beta1 = beta1\n   445→\n   446→        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n   447→        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - device_beta1)\n   448→\n   449→        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n   450→        if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n   451→            if beta2.requires_grad:\n   452→                # Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n   453→                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n   454→                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n   455→                #           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n   456→                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n   457→                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n   458→                # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\n   459→                # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\n   460→                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n   461→            else:\n   462→                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n   463→                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n   464→                )\n   465→        else:\n   466→            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   467→\n   468→        if capturable or differentiable:\n   469→            step = step_t\n   470→\n   471→            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n   472→            if differentiable and isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n   473→                if beta1.requires_grad:\n   474→                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1 ** step.clone()\n   475→                else:\n   476→                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n   477→            else:\n   478→                bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n   479→\n   480→            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n   481→            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n   482→                if beta2.requires_grad:\n   483→                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n   484→                else:\n   485→                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n   486→            else:\n   487→                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n   488→\n   489→            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n   490→            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n   491→\n   492→            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n   493→\n   494→            if amsgrad:\n   495→                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n   496→                if differentiable:\n   497→                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n   498→                else:\n   499→                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n   500→\n   501→                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n   502→\n   503→                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n   504→                # Folds in (admittedly ugly) 1-elem step_size math here to avoid extra param-set-sized read+write\n   505→                # (can't fold it into addcdiv_ below because addcdiv_ requires value is a Number, not a Tensor)\n   506→                denom = (\n   507→                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n   508→                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n   509→            else:\n   510→                denom = (\n   511→                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n   512→                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n   513→\n   514→            if differentiable:\n   515→                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n   516→            else:\n   517→                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n   518→        else:\n   519→            step = _get_value(step_t)\n   520→\n   521→            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n   522→            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n   523→\n   524→            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n   525→\n   526→            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n   527→\n   528→            if amsgrad:\n   529→                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n   530→                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n   531→\n   532→                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n   533→                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n   534→            else:\n   535→                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n   536→\n   537→            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   538→\n   539→        # Lastly, switch back to complex view\n   540→        if amsgrad and torch.is_complex(params[i]):\n   541→            max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_complex(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n   542→\n   543→\n   544→def _multi_tensor_adam(\n   545→    params: list[Tensor],\n   546→    grads: list[Tensor],\n   547→    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n   548→    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   549→    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   550→    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n   551→    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n   552→    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n   553→    *,\n   554→    amsgrad: bool,\n   555→    has_complex: bool,\n   556→    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n   557→    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n   558→    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n   559→    weight_decay: float,\n   560→    eps: float,\n   561→    maximize: bool,\n   562→    capturable: bool,\n   563→    differentiable: bool,\n   564→    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n   565→):\n   566→    if len(params) == 0:\n   567→        return\n   568→\n   569→    if isinstance(lr, Tensor):\n   570→        if not capturable:\n   571→            raise RuntimeError(\n   572→                \"lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n   573→            )\n   574→        if lr.numel() != 1:\n   575→            raise ValueError(\"Tensor lr must be 1-element\")\n   576→\n   577→    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n   578→        if not capturable:\n   579→            raise ValueError(\n   580→                \"beta1 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n   581→            )\n   582→        if beta1.numel() != 1:\n   583→            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta1 must be 1-element\")\n   584→\n   585→    if isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n   586→        if not capturable:\n   587→            raise ValueError(\n   588→                \"beta2 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n   589→            )\n   590→        if beta2.numel() != 1:\n   591→            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta2 must be 1-element\")\n   592→\n   593→    # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n   594→    if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n   595→        capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices(\n   596→            supports_xla=False\n   597→        )\n   598→        assert all(\n   599→            p.device.type == step.device.type\n   600→            and p.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n   601→            for p, step in zip(params, state_steps)\n   602→        ), (\n   603→            f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n   604→        )\n   605→\n   606→    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n   607→\n   608→    assert not differentiable, \"_foreach ops don't support autograd\"\n   609→\n   610→    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n   611→    # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n   612→\n   613→    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n   614→        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n   615→    )\n   616→\n   617→    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n   618→    # treating it as a scalar.\n   619→    beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDict] = (  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n   620→        {beta1.device: beta1}\n   621→        if isinstance(beta1, Tensor) and str(beta1.device) != \"cpu\"\n   622→        else None\n   623→    )\n   624→\n   625→    for (\n   626→        device_params_,\n   627→        device_grads_,\n   628→        device_exp_avgs_,\n   629→        device_exp_avg_sqs_,\n   630→        device_max_exp_avg_sqs_,\n   631→        device_state_steps_,\n   632→    ), _ in grouped_tensors.values():\n   633→        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n   634→        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n   635→        device_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avgs_)\n   636→        device_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avg_sqs_)\n   637→        device_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], device_state_steps_)\n   638→\n   639→        device = device_params[0].device\n   640→        if beta1_dict is not None and device not in beta1_dict:\n   641→            beta1_dict[device] = beta1.to(device=device, non_blocking=True)  # type: ignore[union-attr, attr-defined]\n   642→\n   643→        device_beta1 = beta1_dict[device] if beta1_dict else beta1\n   644→\n   645→        # Handle complex parameters\n   646→        if has_complex:\n   647→            if amsgrad:\n   648→                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n   649→                _view_as_real(\n   650→                    device_params,\n   651→                    device_grads,\n   652→                    device_exp_avgs,\n   653→                    device_exp_avg_sqs,\n   654→                    device_max_exp_avg_sqs,\n   655→                )\n   656→            else:\n   657→                _view_as_real(\n   658→                    device_params, device_grads, device_exp_avgs, device_exp_avg_sqs\n   659→                )\n   660→\n   661→        if maximize:\n   662→            device_grads = torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n   663→\n   664→        # Update steps\n   665→        # If steps are on CPU, foreach will fall back to the slow path, which is a for-loop calling t.add(1) over\n   666→        # and over. 1 will then be wrapped into a Tensor over and over again, which is slower than if we just\n   667→        # wrapped it once now. The alpha is required to assure we go to the right overload.\n   668→        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and device_state_steps[0].is_cpu:\n   669→            torch._foreach_add_(\n   670→                device_state_steps, torch.tensor(1.0, device=\"cpu\"), alpha=1.0\n   671→            )\n   672→        else:\n   673→            torch._foreach_add_(device_state_steps, 1)\n   674→\n   675→        if weight_decay != 0:\n   676→            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n   677→                # Perform stepweight decay\n   678→                torch._foreach_mul_(device_params, 1 - lr * weight_decay)\n   679→            else:\n   680→                # Reuse the intermediate memory (device_grads) already allocated for maximize\n   681→                if maximize:\n   682→                    torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)\n   683→                else:\n   684→                    device_grads = torch._foreach_add(  # type: ignore[assignment]\n   685→                        device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay\n   686→                    )\n   687→\n   688→        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n   689→        # Use device beta1 if beta1 is a tensor to ensure all\n   690→        # tensors are on the same device\n   691→        torch._foreach_lerp_(\n   692→            device_exp_avgs, device_grads, cast(float, 1 - device_beta1)\n   693→        )\n   694→\n   695→        torch._foreach_mul_(device_exp_avg_sqs, beta2)\n   696→\n   697→        # Due to the strictness of the _foreach_addcmul API, we can't have a single\n   698→        # tensor scalar as the scalar arg (only python number is supported there)\n   699→        # as a result, separate out the value mul\n   700→        # Filed https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/139795\n   701→        if isinstance(beta2, torch.Tensor):\n   702→            scaled_device_grads = torch._foreach_mul(device_grads, 1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n   703→            value = 1.0\n   704→        else:\n   705→            scaled_device_grads = device_grads  # type: ignore[assignment]\n   706→            value = 1 - beta2\n   707→\n   708→        torch._foreach_addcmul_(\n   709→            device_exp_avg_sqs, scaled_device_grads, device_grads, value\n   710→        )\n   711→\n   712→        # Delete the local intermediate(s) since they won't be used anymore to save on peak memory\n   713→        del device_grads\n   714→        del scaled_device_grads\n   715→\n   716→        bias_correction1: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n   717→        bias_correction2: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n   718→        bias_correction2_sqrt: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n   719→\n   720→        if capturable:\n   721→            bias_correction1 = torch._foreach_pow(beta1, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   722→            bias_correction2 = torch._foreach_pow(beta2, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   723→            # foreach_sub doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\n   724→            torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction1, 1)\n   725→            torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction2, 1)\n   726→            # we do not negate bias_correction1 as it'll need to be negated later anyway\n   727→            torch._foreach_neg_(bias_correction2)\n   728→\n   729→            # foreach_div doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\n   730→            torch._foreach_div_(bias_correction1, lr)\n   731→            torch._foreach_reciprocal_(bias_correction1)\n   732→\n   733→            torch._foreach_sqrt_(bias_correction2)\n   734→\n   735→            # Re-assign for clarity as we maintain minimal intermediates: we'll have\n   736→            # step_size = - lr / (1 - beta1 ^ t) where t = num_steps\n   737→            # bias_correction2_sqrt = sqrt(1 - beta2 ^ t)\n   738→            step_size = bias_correction1\n   739→            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2\n   740→\n   741→            if amsgrad:\n   742→                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n   743→                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n   744→                torch._foreach_maximum_(device_max_exp_avg_sqs, device_exp_avg_sqs)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n   745→\n   746→                # Set intermediate to the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient when amsgrad\n   747→                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_max_exp_avg_sqs)\n   748→            else:\n   749→                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_exp_avg_sqs)\n   750→\n   751→            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, bias_correction2_sqrt)\n   752→            torch._foreach_add_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, eps)\n   753→            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, step_size)\n   754→\n   755→            # at this point, exp_avg_sq_sqrt = - (1 - beta^t) * [sqrt(exp_avg_sq / (1 - beta2^t)) + eps] / lr\n   756→            torch._foreach_addcdiv_(device_params, device_exp_avgs, exp_avg_sq_sqrt)\n   757→        else:\n   758→            bias_correction1 = [\n   759→                1 - beta1 ** _get_value(step) for step in device_state_steps\n   760→            ]\n   761→            bias_correction2 = [\n   762→                1 - beta2 ** _get_value(step) for step in device_state_steps\n   763→            ]\n   764→\n   765→            step_size = _stack_if_compiling([(lr / bc) * -1 for bc in bias_correction1])\n   766→\n   767→            bias_correction2_sqrt = [bc**0.5 for bc in bias_correction2]  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   768→\n   769→            if amsgrad:\n   770→                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n   771→                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n   772→                torch._foreach_maximum_(device_max_exp_avg_sqs, device_exp_avg_sqs)\n   773→\n   774→                # r\"\"\"Implements Adam algorithm.\n\n    .. math::\n       \\begin{aligned}\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\beta_1, \\beta_2\n                \\text{ (betas)},\\theta_0 \\text{ (params)},f(\\theta) \\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{13mm}      \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},  \\: \\textit{amsgrad},\n                \\:\\textit{maximize},  \\: \\epsilon \\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\n            &\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( first moment)},\n                v_0\\leftarrow 0 \\text{ (second moment)},\\: v_0^{max}\\leftarrow 0          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                         \\\\\n\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   -\\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   \\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\lambda \\neq 0                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda  \\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\widehat{m_t} \\leftarrow   m_t/\\big(1-\\beta_1^t \\big)                   \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\leftarrow \\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)              \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow   v_t/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1} - \\gamma \\widehat{m_t}/\n                \\big(\\sqrt{\\widehat{v_t}} + \\epsilon \\big)                                       \\\\\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\n            is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\n            LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\n        betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n            running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n        eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n            numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\n            equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\n            decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\n        amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\n            algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\n            (default: False)\n        {_foreach_doc}\n        {_maximize_doc}\n        {_capturable_doc}\n        {_differentiable_doc}\n        {_fused_doc}\n    .. Note::\n        A prototype implementation of Adam and AdamW for MPS supports `torch.float32` and `torch.float16`.\n    .. _Adam\\: A Method for Stochastic Optimization:\n        https://arxiv.org/abs/1412.6980\n    .. _On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond:\n        https://openreview.net/forum?id=ryQu7f-RZ\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef _single_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    if torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        # this assert is due to JIT being dumb and not realizing that the ops below\n        # have overloads to handle both float and Tensor lrs, so we just assert it's\n        # a float since most people using JIT are using floats\n        assert isinstance(lr, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta1, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta2, float)\n    else:\n        lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n        # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    # Note: ensure type declaration is under conditional check for isinstance\n    # or else torchscript will get cranky about the DeviceDict type.\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDtypeDict] = {(beta1.device, beta1.dtype): beta1}\n    else:\n        beta1_dict = None\n\n    for i, param in enumerate(params):\n        grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\n        exp_avg = exp_avgs[i]\n        exp_avg_sq = exp_avg_sqs[i]\n        step_t = state_steps[i]\n\n        # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n            capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices()\n            assert (\n                param.device.type == step_t.device.type\n                and param.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            ), (\n                f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n            )\n\n        # update step\n        step_t += 1\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n                if differentiable and isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n                    if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n                        grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n                    else:\n                        grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n\n        if torch.is_complex(param):\n            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n            if amsgrad:\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_real(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n\n        device = param.device\n\n        if beta1_dict is not None:\n            dtype = param.dtype  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n\n            # cast to workaround https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/140601\n            key = (device, dtype)\n            if key not in beta1_dict:\n                beta1_dict[key] = beta1.to(  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n                    device=device, dtype=dtype, non_blocking=True\n                )\n\n            device_beta1: Union[float, Tensor] = beta1_dict[key]\n        else:\n            device_beta1 = beta1\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - device_beta1)\n\n        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n        if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n            if beta2.requires_grad:\n                # Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                #           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\n                # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\n                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n                )\n        else:\n            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        if capturable or differentiable:\n            step = step_t\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n                if beta1.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n                if beta2.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                if differentiable:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n                else:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n\n                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                # Folds in (admittedly ugly) 1-elem step_size math here to avoid extra param-set-sized read+write\n                # (can't fold it into addcdiv_ below because addcdiv_ requires value is a Number, not a Tensor)\n                denom = (\n                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n            else:\n                denom = (\n                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n\n            if differentiable:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n            else:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n        else:\n            step = _get_value(step_t)\n\n            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n            else:\n                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n\n            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        # Lastly, switch back to complex view\n        if amsgrad and torch.is_complex(params[i]):\n            max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_complex(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n\ndef _multi_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n\n    if isinstance(lr, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise RuntimeError(\n                \"lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if lr.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor lr must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta1 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta1.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta1 must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta2 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta2.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta2 must be 1-element\")\n\n    # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n    if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n        capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices(\n            supports_xla=False\n        )\n        assert all(\n            p.device.type == step.device.type\n            and p.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            for p, step in zip(params, state_steps)\n        ), (\n            f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n        )\n\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    assert not differentiable, \"_foreach ops don't support autograd\"\n\n    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n    # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n    )\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDict] = (  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n        {beta1.device: beta1}\n        if isinstance(beta1, Tensor) and str(beta1.device) != \"cpu\"\n        else None\n    )\n\n    for (\n        device_params_,\n        device_grads_,\n        device_exp_avgs_,\n        device_exp_avg_sqs_,\n        device_max_exp_avg_sqs_,\n        device_state_steps_,\n    ), _ in grouped_tensors.values():\n        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n        device_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avgs_)\n        device_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avg_sqs_)\n        device_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], device_state_steps_)\n\n        device = device_params[0].device\n        if beta1_dict is not None and device not in beta1_dict:\n            beta1_dict[device] = beta1.to(device=device, non_blocking=True)  # type: ignore[union-attr, attr-defined]\n\n        device_beta1 = beta1_dict[device] if beta1_dict else beta1\n\n        # Handle complex parameters\n        if has_complex:\n            if amsgrad:\n                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n                _view_as_real(\n                    device_params,\n                    device_grads,\n                    device_exp_avgs,\n                    device_exp_avg_sqs,\n                    device_max_exp_avg_sqs,\n                )\n            else:\n                _view_as_real(\n                    device_params, device_grads, device_exp_avgs, device_exp_avg_sqs\n                )\n\n        if maximize:\n            device_grads = torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n\n        # Update steps\n        # If steps are on CPU, foreach will fall back to the slow path, which is a for-loop calling t.add(1) over\n        # and over. 1 will then be wrapped into a Tensor over and over again, which is slower than if we just\n        # wrapped it once now. The alpha is required to assure we go to the right overload.\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and device_state_steps[0].is_cpu:\n            torch._foreach_add_(\n                device_state_steps, torch.tensor(1.0, device=\"cpu\"), alpha=1.0\n            )\n        else:\n            torch._foreach_add_(device_state_steps, 1)\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                torch._foreach_mul_(device_params, 1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Reuse the intermediate memory (device_grads) already allocated for maximize\n                if maximize:\n                    torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    device_grads = torch._foreach_add(  # type: ignore[assignment]\n                        device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay\n                    )\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        # Use device beta1 if beta1 is a tensor to ensure all\n        # tensors are on the same device\n        torch._foreach_lerp_(\n            device_exp_avgs, device_grads, cast(float, 1 - device_beta1)\n        )\n\n        torch._foreach_mul_(device_exp_avg_sqs, beta2)\n\n        # Due to the strictness of the _foreach_addcmul API, we can't have a single\n        # tensor scalar as the scalar arg (only python number is supported there)\n        # as a result, separate out the value mul\n        # Filed https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/139795\n        if isinstance(beta2, torch.Tensor):\n            scaled_device_grads = torch._foreach_mul(device_grads, 1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n            value = 1.0\n        else:\n            scaled_device_grads = device_grads  # type: ignore[assignment]\n            value = 1 - beta2\n\n        torch._foreach_addcmul_(\n            device_exp_avg_sqs, scaled_device_grads, device_grads, value\n        )\n\n        # Delete the local intermediate(s) since they won't be used anymore to save on peak memory\n        del device_grads\n        del scaled_device_grads\n\n        bias_correction1: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n        bias_correction2: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n        bias_correction2_sqrt: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n\n        if capturable:\n            bias_correction1 = torch._foreach_pow(beta1, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            bias_correction2 = torch._foreach_pow(beta2, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            # foreach_sub doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\n            torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction1, 1)\n            torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction2, 1)\n            # we do not negate bias_correction1 as it'll need to be negated later anyway\n            torch._foreach_neg_(bias_correction2)\n\n            # foreach_div doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\n            torch._foreach_div_(bias_correction1, lr)\n            torch._foreach_reciprocal_(bias_correction1)\n\n            torch._foreach_sqrt_(bias_correction2)\n\n            # Re-assign for clarity as we maintain minimal intermediates: we'll have\n            # step_size = - lr / (1 - beta1 ^ t) where t = num_steps\n            # bias_correction2_sqrt = sqrt(1 - beta2 ^ t)\n            step_size = bias_correction1\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch._foreach_maximum_(device_max_exp_avg_sqs, device_exp_avg_sqs)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n\n                # Set intermediate to the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient when amsgrad\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_max_exp_avg_sqs)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_exp_avg_sqs)\n\n            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, bias_correction2_sqrt)\n            torch._foreach_add_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, eps)\n            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, step_size)\n\n            # at this point, exp_avg_sq_sqrt = - (1 - beta^t) * [sqrt(exp_avg_sq / (1 - beta2^t)) + eps] / lr\n            torch._foreach_addcdiv_(device_params, device_exp_avgs, exp_avg_sq_sqrt)\n        else:\n            bias_correction1 = [\n                1 - beta1 ** _get_value(step) for step in device_state_steps\n            ]\n            bias_correction2 = [\n                1 - beta2 ** _get_value(step) for step in device_state_steps\n            ]\n\n            step_size = _stack_if_compiling([(lr / bc) * -1 for bc in bias_correction1])\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = [bc**0.5 for bc in bias_correction2]  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch._foreach_maximum_(device_max_exp_avg_sqs, device_exp_avg_sqs)\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_max_exp_avg_sqs)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_exp_avg_sqs)\n\n            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, bias_correction2_sqrt)\n            torch._foreach_add_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, eps)\n            torch._foreach_addcdiv_(\n                device_params,\n                device_exp_avgs,\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt,\n                step_size,  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            )\n\n\ndef _fused_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,  # Needed for consistency.\n    beta1: float,\n    beta2: float,\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,  # Needed for consistency.\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n) -> None:\n    if not params:\n        return\n    if differentiable:\n        raise RuntimeError(\"Adam with fused=True does not support differentiable=True\")\n\n    grad_scale_dict: DeviceDict = (\n        {grad_scale.device: grad_scale} if grad_scale is not None else {}\n    )\n    found_inf_dict: DeviceDict = (\n        {found_inf.device: found_inf} if found_inf is not None else {}\n    )\n\n    # We only shuffle around the lr when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    lr_dict: Optional[DeviceDict] = (\n        {lr.device: lr} if isinstance(lr, Tensor) and str(lr.device) != \"cpu\" else None\n    )\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n    )\n    for (device, _), (\n        (\n            device_params_,\n            device_grads_,\n            device_exp_avgs_,\n            device_exp_avg_sqs_,\n            device_max_exp_avg_sqs,\n            device_state_steps_,\n        ),\n        _,\n    ) in grouped_tensors.items():\n        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n        device_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avgs_)\n        device_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avg_sqs_)\n        device_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], device_state_steps_)\n\n        device_grad_scale, device_found_inf = None, None\n        if grad_scale is not None:\n            device_grad_scale = grad_scale_dict.setdefault(\n                device, grad_scale.to(device, non_blocking=True)\n            )\n        if found_inf is not None:\n            device_found_inf = found_inf_dict.setdefault(\n                device, found_inf.to(device, non_blocking=True)\n            )\n        if lr_dict is not None and device not in lr_dict:\n            lr_dict[device] = lr.to(device=device, non_blocking=True)  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n            lr = lr_dict[device]\n        torch._foreach_add_(device_state_steps, 1)\n        func = torch._fused_adam_ if not decoupled_weight_decay else torch._fused_adamw_\n        func(\n            device_params,\n            device_grads,\n            device_exp_avgs,\n            device_exp_avg_sqs,\n            device_max_exp_avg_sqs,  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            device_state_steps,\n            amsgrad=amsgrad,\n            lr=lr,  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            beta1=beta1,\n            beta2=beta2,\n            weight_decay=weight_decay,\n            eps=eps,\n            maximize=maximize,\n            grad_scale=device_grad_scale,\n            found_inf=device_found_inf,\n        )\n        if device_found_inf is not None:\n            torch._foreach_sub_(\n                device_state_steps, [device_found_inf] * len(device_state_steps)\n            )\n\n\n@_disable_dynamo_if_unsupported(single_tensor_fn=_single_tensor_adam)\ndef adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\n    # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\n    foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\n    capturable: bool = False,\n    differentiable: bool = False,\n    fused: Optional[bool] = None,\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    has_complex: bool = False,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool = False,\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    beta1: float,\n    beta2: float,\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n):\n    r\"\"\"Functional API that performs Adam algorithm computation.\n\n    See :class:`~torch.optim.Adam` for details.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. We only want to change\n    # the default when neither have been user-specified. Note that we default to foreach\n    # and pass False to use_fused. This is not a mistake--we want to give the fused impl\n    # bake-in time before making it the default, even if it is typically faster.\n    if fused is None and foreach is None:\n        _, foreach = _default_to_fused_or_foreach(\n            params, differentiable, use_fused=False\n        )\n        # Common Code Patterns (Appearing in 9-11 optimizers)\n\n#### Pattern A: Empty Parameters Check (10/11 optimizers)\n```python\nif len(params) == 0:\n    return\n```\n**Appears in:** SGD, Adam, Adamax, Adagrad, RAdam, RMSProp, Nadam, ASGD, Rprop, AdaDelta\n**Missing in:** None (all have it, but AdaFactor has it at line 475)\n\n#### Pattern B: Learning Rate Scalar Conversion (10/11 optimizers)\n```python\nlr = _to_scalar(lr)\n```\n**Appears in:** SGD, Adam, Adamax, Adagrad, RAdam, RMSProp, Nadam, ASGD, AdaDelta, AdaFactor\n**Notes:** Converts tensor LR to scalar or keeps as-is; ensures compatibility with foreach ops\n\n#### Pattern C: Device/Dtype Grouping (11/11 optimizers)\n```python\ngrouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n    [params, grads, ...],\n    with_indices=True,  # Optional\n)\nfor (device_params, device_grads, ...), [indices] in grouped_tensors.values():\n    ...\n```\n**Appears in:** ALL optimizers\n**Special case:** AdaFactor uses `_group_tensors_by_device_dtype_and_is_multidim()` instead\n\n#### Pattern D: State Step Increment (11/11 optimizers)\n```python\n# If steps are on CPU, foreach will fall back to the slow path...\nif not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and grouped_state_steps[0].is_cpu:\n    torch._foreach_add_(\n        grouped_state_steps, torch.tensor(1.0, device=\"cpu\"), alpha=1.0\n    )\nelse:\n    torch._foreach_add_(grouped_state_steps, 1)\n```\n**Appears in:** ALL optimizers (identical pattern)\n**Length:** 6 lines with identical comment (word-for-word identical)\n\n#### Pattern E: Maximize Handling - Negate Gradients (11/11 optimizers)\n```python\nif maximize:\n    device_grads = torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n```\n**Appears in:** ALL optimizers\n**Notes:** Allows maximization by negating gradients. Assignment creates new list/tuple.\n\n#### Pattern F: Weight Decay (10/11 optimizers)\n```python\nif weight_decay != 0:\n    if maximize:\n        # Reuse intermediate memory\n        torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)\n    else:\n        device_grads = torch._foreach_add(\n            device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay\n        )\n```\n**Appears in:** SGD, Adam, Adamax, Adagrad, RAdam, RMSProp, Nadam, ASGD, AdaDelta\n**Variations:** \n- AdaFactor uses decoupled weight decay: `torch._foreach_mul_(device_params, 1 - lr * weight_decay)`\n- RAdam and Nadam also support `decoupled_weight_decay` parameter\n\n#### Pattern G: Complex Parameter Handling (10/11 optimizers)\n```python\nif has_complex:\n    _view_as_real(\n        device_params, device_grads, device_square_avgs, ...\n    )\n```\n**Appears in:** Adam, Adamax, Adagrad, RAdam, RMSProp, Nadam, ASGD, Rprop, AdaDelta, AdaFactor\n**Missing in:** SGD\n**Helper function location:** `/workspace/torch/optim/optimizer.py:203`\n\n#### Pattern H: Capturable Assertions (9/11 optimizers)\n```python\nif not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n    capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices(supports_xla=False)\n    assert all(\n        p.device.type == step.device.type\n        and p.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n        for p, step in zip(params, state_steps)\n    ), (\n        f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices...\"\n    )\n```\n**Appears in:** Adam, Adamax, RAdam, RMSProp, Nadam, ASGD, Rprop, AdaDelta, AdaFactor\n**Missing in:** SGD, Adagrad\n**Notes:** Validates device compatibility for CUDA graphs\n\n#### Pattern I: Sparse Gradient Handling (2/11 optimizers)\n```python\ndevice_has_sparse_grad = has_sparse_grad and any(\n    grad.is_sparse for grad in device_grads\n)\n\nif device_has_sparse_grad:\n    # Fall back to single-tensor implementation\n    _single_tensor_adagrad(\n        device_params, device_grads, ..., has_sparse_grad=True\n    )\n    continue\n```\n**Appears in:** SGD, Adagrad\n**Notes:** Foreach ops don't support sparse tensors; must fall back to loop\n\n#### Pattern J: Differentiability Assertion (11/11 optimizers)\n```python\nassert not differentiable, \"_foreach ops don't support autograd\"\n```\n**Appears in:** All except SGD (missing assertion)\n**Location in code:** Typically near beginning, before main logic\n\n#### Pattern K: Parameter Validation for Tensor Hyperparameters (3/11 optimizers)\n```python\nif isinstance(lr, Tensor):\n    if not capturable:\n        raise RuntimeError(...)\n    if lr.numel() != 1:\n        raise ValueError(\"Tensor lr must be 1-element\")\n```\n**Appears in:** Adam (for beta1, beta2, lr)\n**Missing in:** Most other optimizers that support tensor LR\n**Notes:** Adam is stricter about tensor hyperparameters\n\n#### Pattern L: Tensor LR Handling in Parameter Update (2/11 optimizers)\n```python\nif capturable and isinstance(lr, torch.Tensor):\n    grads_x_lr = torch._foreach_mul(device_grads, -lr)\n    torch._foreach_add_(device_params, grads_x_lr)\nelse:\n    torch._foreach_add_(device_params, device_grads, alpha=-lr)\n```\n**Appears in:** SGD, RMSProp\n**Notes:** Workaround for torch.compile + capturable requiring explicit tensor operations\n\n### 3. Algorithm-Specific Code Patterns (Should Stay in Each Optimizer)\n\n#### SGD-specific:\n- Momentum buffer handling with `all_states_with_momentum_buffer` check\n- Nesterov momentum special case: `torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, bufs, alpha=momentum)`\n\n#### Adam-specific:\n- Complex parameter view_as_real handling with amsgrad branching\n- Beta1 device dict: `beta1_dict = {beta1.device: beta1} if isinstance(beta1, Tensor)...`\n- State step increment with CPU tensor wrapping\n- EMA updates: `torch._foreach_lerp_(device_exp_avgs, device_grads, 1 - device_beta1)`\n\n#### Adamax-specific:\n- Exponential infinity norm: `torch._foreach_maximum_(grouped_exp_infs, grouped_grads)`\n- Bias correction with capturable branches (different computation for scalar vs tensor step)\n- Addcdiv with step_size multiplication\n\n#### Adagrad-specific:\n- Learning rate decay: `minus_clr = [-lr / (1 + (_get_value(step) - 1) * lr_decay) for step in ...]`\n- State sum accumulation: `torch._foreach_addcmul_(device_state_sums, device_grads, device_grads, value=1)`\n\n#### RAdam-specific:\n- Rho infinity calculation: `rho_inf = 2 / (1 - beta2) - 1`\n- Complex bias correction and rho_t calculation with capturable branching\n- Conditional rectification: `rect = [torch.where(rho_t > 5.0, n, 0.0) for n, rho_t in zip(num, rho_t_list)]`\n\n#### RMSProp-specific:\n- Centered vs non-centered branches\n- Momentum buffer optional handling\n- Two different update paths based on momentum presence\n\n#### Nadam-specific:\n- Momentum decay exponential: `0.96 ** (_get_value(step) * momentum_decay)`\n- Mu and mu_next calculations\n- Bias correction sqrt computation\n\n#### ASGD-specific:\n- Weight decay + lambd handling: `intermediate = torch._foreach_add(..., alpha=lambd)`\n- Parameter update with eta scaling: `torch._foreach_addcmul_(grouped_params, intermediate, grouped_etas, value=-1)`\n- No state_steps update (only marks as in param update path)\n\n#### Rprop-specific:\n- Sign-based step size adjustment (unusual algorithm)\n- Sign multiplication then conditional clamping\n- No weight decay, no learning rate scaling\n\n#### AdaDelta-specific:\n- RMS computation without learning rate: `std = torch._foreach_add(device_square_avgs, eps)`\n- Update accumulation: `torch._foreach_mul_(device_acc_deltas, rho)`\n- Capturable tensor LR handling in update\n\n#### AdaFactor-specific:\n- Custom grouping: `_group_tensors_by_device_dtype_and_is_multidim()`\n- Multidimensional factorization (row_vars, col_vars vs variance)\n- Parameter norm-based alpha scaling\n- Beta2 decay computation\n\n### 4.
